## <a name="windows-server-2003-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="fe174-722">Atributos do Windows Server 2003 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fe174-722">Windows Server 2003 R2 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fe174-723">Essa classe contém os seguintes atributos para o Windows Server 2003 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fe174-723">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2003 R2:</span></span>
